<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notes">Notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Southern_Ocean&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="reflist" style="list-style-type: decimal;">
<ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-5"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-5">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Also a translation of its former <a href="/wiki/French_language" title="French language">French</a> name (<i><span lang="fr" xml:lang="fr">Grand Oc√©an Austral</span></i>) in reference to its position below the <a href="/wiki/Pacific_Ocean" title="Pacific Ocean">Pacific</a>, the "<span lang="fr" xml:lang="fr">Grand Oc√©an</span>".</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-7"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-7">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Used by <a href="/wiki/Joseph_Dalton_Hooker" title="Joseph Dalton Hooker">Dr¬†Hooker</a> in his accounts of his Antarctic voyages.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6"><a href="#cite_note-6">[5]</a></sup> Also a translation of the ocean's <a href="/wiki/Japanese_language" title="Japanese language">Japanese</a> name <i>Nankyoku Kai</i> (<span lang="jp" xml:lang="jp"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/%E5%8D%97%E6%A5%B5%E6%B5%B7" title="wikt:ÂçóÊ•µÊµ∑">ÂçóÊ•µÊµ∑</a></span>).</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-8"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-8">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Also a translation of the ocean's <a href="/wiki/Chinese_language" title="Chinese language">Chinese</a> name <i>N√°nbƒ´ng Y√°ng</i> (<span lang="zh" xml:lang="zh"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/%E5%8D%97%E5%86%B0%E6%B4%8B" title="wikt:ÂçóÂÜ∞Ê¥ã">ÂçóÂÜ∞Ê¥ã</a></span>).</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-9"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-9">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Historic names include the "<b>South Sea</b>",<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-robinhood_3-0"><a href="#cite_note-robinhood-3">[3]</a></sup> the "<b>Great Southern Ocean</b>",<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTE.27.27EB.27.271911_4-0"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTE.27.27EB.27.271911-4">[4]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5"><a href="#cite_note-5">[note 1]</a></sup> the "<b>South Polar Ocean</b>" or "<b>South-Polar Ocean</b>",<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7"><a href="#cite_note-7">[note 2]</a></sup> and the "<b>Southern Icy Ocean</b>".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-robinhood_3-1"><a href="#cite_note-robinhood-3">[3]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8"><a href="#cite_note-8">[note 3]</a></sup></span></li>
<li id="cite_note-13"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-13">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">A subsidiary of <a href="/wiki/Encyclop%C3%A6dia_Britannica,_Inc." title="Encyclop√¶dia Britannica, Inc.">Encyclop√¶dia Britannica, Inc.</a></span></li>
<li id="cite_note-19"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-19">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">In violation of their <i>Style Guide</i>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTENGS2014_2-2"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTENGS2014-2">[2]</a></sup> however, some of National Geographic's online news blogs do use the term.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nationalgeographic_18-0"><a href="#cite_note-nationalgeographic-18">[13]</a></sup></span></li>
<li id="cite_note-67"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-67">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Reservation by Norway: Norway recognizes the name <a href="/wiki/King_Haakon_VII_Sea" title="King Haakon VII Sea">Kong H√•kon VII Hav</a> which covers the sea area adjacent to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Dronning_Maud_Land" title="Dronning Maud Land">Dronning Maud Land</a> and stretching from 20¬∞W to 45¬∞E.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-IHO2002_34-2"><a href="#cite_note-IHO2002-34">[28]</a></sup></span></li>
<li id="cite_note-68"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-68">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The <a href="/wiki/Drake_Passage" title="Drake Passage">Drake Passage</a> is situated between the southern and eastern extremities of <a href="/wiki/South_America" title="South America">South America</a> and the <a href="/wiki/South_Shetland_Islands" title="South Shetland Islands">South Shetland Islands</a>, lying north of the <a href="/wiki/Antarctic_Peninsula" title="Antarctic Peninsula">Antarctic Peninsula</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Scotia_Sea" title="Scotia Sea">Scotia Sea</a> is an area defined by the southeastern extremity of South America and the <a href="/wiki/South_Shetland_Islands" title="South Shetland Islands">South Shetland Islands</a> on the west and by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/South_Georgia" title="South Georgia">South Georgia</a> and the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/South_Sandwich_Islands" title="South Sandwich Islands">South Sandwich Islands</a> to the north and east. As they extend north of 60¬∞S, Drake Passage and the Scotia Sea are also described as forming part of the <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_Ocean" title="Atlantic Ocean">South Atlantic Ocean</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-IHO2002_34-3"><a href="#cite_note-IHO2002-34">[28]</a></sup></span></li>
</ol>
